<rating>2< /rating><review>I usually have a good experience however I faced unpleasant incidents today:

I donate blood regularly and prior to each donation, I inform the nurse about my veins being too small and that they require a bit of extra attention for a good flow and no bruise later on my skin. The information is usually appreciated and no issues arise.

However, to my surprise today, the nurse who was a big lady and acted inconsiderate with the info I provided for her, enlightened me firmly with some additional information:
‚ÄúIt is a needle, it will go inside your skin, and it will hurt..! So if you think it will not hurt, you better understand, it will!.....‚Äù

I thought she was rude, angry and a bit too violent for the occasion. So I politely requested for her supervisor. (Later I saw the same big nurse laughing loud with other volunteers trying to look all sweet, friendly and fun - no one else was laughing as loud and as long!)

The supervisor came to me and she was obviously told by the big lady that I was a volunteer scared of needles. The supervisor tried to nicely explain there WILL be some pain! She also checked my arms and told me she was surprised why I have had issues before. As if I had imagined those issues about small veins - perhaps because I was scared of needles?!

Fast forward, I left half an later without being able to donate, after two nurses tried and tried to get blood flow from that small vein I had explained to them but they had not taken it seriously.
They put the needle in and out and moved it in my skin several times looking for the vein asking me if it was painful?! The big nurse had come to help and she could not get the blood flow either. Eventually they gave up.

A friendly note to the Red Cross -

All the consultation prior to the donation is to minimize complications. Please take comments from the volunteers seriously. If I inform you my veins are small, it does not mean I am scared of needles. It simply means ‚Äúmy veins are small‚Äù and I know it from experience. Is it impossible to draw blood from my veins? Please don‚Äôt give the lecture that all your nurses are equally good. See what happened today? So we did that, and then we walked past a shed with a huge sign 'pesticides, keep out.' When we went to pay, I asked the girl if the apples are organic and she literally said 'I don't know what that means.' Seriously!? <user>114771828279526962867< /user><Name>Allen B.</Name><Date>1422244576331< /Date><Rate>1<//Rate>< Text>
So Disappointing.

This review is based on the overall experience. Our 11 year old son, after a previous visit to this gym, requested his birthday party be kept at this place. We called the Gym in advance to reserve, and were told that the reservation can only be done online and assured us it is easy, safe and secured (questionable). Setup the reservation online paying the deposit, and when we called the day before the event to ask questions regarding bringing in the pizza and cake, we were told "There is NO reservation!", and that there is nothing that can be done at this time. We had invited 16 kids to come from Lafayette and had no place to go. After calling back, the reservation was found, however made at Fresno Gym. We never inquired about any other locations and made the reservation on their site without getting any options to choose a different location. Now that the reservation was found, we are told that we still cannot come because they do not have staff. We offered to do ropes and we were told to come late that day for training. Once the staff part was resolved, we were told that they do not have a room to do the party in. After insisting for awhile, they offered their yoga classroom. Once we saw it we understood their hesitation... The room was smelling terrible and felt dirty and the chairs they provided looked like they were retrieved from a garbage bin as well as not enough of them. Dirty, ugly looking, or even smaller size. We had to ask for someone to do something about that smell so that we can bring the kids and have them fed. The check in process was slow, unpleasant and disorganized. We were embarrassed in front of the parents dropping of their children but for the staff it seemed normal. Most kids in our party within the hour and a half provided, they did the claim once or twice due to the overcrowding and long wait times. We were not at ease with the instructors that told 8-10 year old kids to claim the big boulders without the ropes. Three instructors were supposed to be assigned to our group, however we only saw one active and assumed that two other ones were talking to each other by the smaller boulders intended for the younger kids. Most staff was unpleasant to talk to or was talking to the kids in a "somewhat rude" and inpatient manner without explaining what was that they did wrong.

The amount of stress that this particular part of our son's birthday celebration put on us was not worth the little fun the Gym provides. We believe it may be a great place to work out or claim but by no means they are ready or willing to host and welcome a group of kids coming all at once.< /Text>

< user>
116606274931669213780< /user>
<user_name>Troy Tiscareno</user_name>< time>
1371532322587< /time>
<rate>3<//rate>< text>
Dairy Queen isn't what I normally think of when I want a burger meal, but some friends and I happened to be nearby and hungry, and decided to give it a try. We were very pleasantly surprised to find a $5 lunch deal for a burger, fries, small soda, and a small Blizzard blended ice cream dessert. You can't beat that!

The burger and fries were better than I expected, being better than average for a fast-food burger, and we got our food quickly. Of course, the big winner was the Blizzard (I went with Heath Bar), which are always delicious.

This is a 50's or 60's era Drive In, so the decor consists of a couple of picnic tables along the side of the building, which are frequently sticky from ice cream. They were pretty clean this day, but you never know what you're going to get.

Bottom line, though: if you want a pretty good fast-food burger lunch at a good price, with a bonus Blizzard, it's worth the bit of extra time and effort to visit DQ.<//text>

< Review>

Okay, so I am normally a patient and understanding person; however, I have reached my limit with this store. Here are the facts:
